<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">您的程序没有生成输出文件可能有以下几个原因：</p>
<ol class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-decimal space-y-2 pl-8" depth="0">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">原代码中的 <code class="bg-text-200/5 
border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.3r
em] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">convert_file</code> 函数是空的（使用了 <code class="bg-text-200/
5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.
3rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">pass</code>），所以虽然程序执行成功了，但实际上没有进行任何文件操作。</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">检查确保：
<ul class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-disc space-y-2 pl-8" depth="1">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">input.txt 文件确实存在于当前目录</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">当前目录有写入权限</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="2">input.txt 文件包含有效的HTML内容</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">您可以这样测试：</p>
<ol class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-decimal space-y-2 pl-8" depth="0">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">确保您的 input.txt 文件中有一些HTML内容，比如：</
li>
</ol>

<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">这样处理后:</p>
<ol class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-decimal space-y-2 pl-8" depth="0">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">用户名会被转换为二级标题格式(##)</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">在Markdown中会更醒目</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="2">不会影响其他内容的转换</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="3">能适应不同的用户名</li>
</ol>
<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">效果大致会是这样:</p>

<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">主要改进：</p>
<ol class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-decimal space-y-2 pl-8" depth="0">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">专门针对用户消息进行处理：<code class="bg-text
-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounde
d-[0.3rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">data-testid="user-message"</code></li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">简化了用户名的识别逻辑</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="2">使用三级标题格式（###）来突出显示用户名</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="3">保留了异常处理和输出提示</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="4">确保文件正确打开和写入</li>
</ol>

<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">主要改进：</p>
<ol class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-decimal space-y-2 pl-8" depth="0">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">全面处理各种内容类型：
<ul class="-mt-1 [li&gt;&amp;]:mt-2 list-disc space-y-2 pl-8" depth="1">
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="0">有序列表 (ol)</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">无序列表 (ul)</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="2">段落文本 (p)</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="3">代码块 (pre)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="1">分别处理每种类型的内容并保持其格式</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="2">确保内容的完整性和顺序</li>
<li class="whitespace-normal break-words" index="3">保留必要的空行和格式</li>
</ol>
<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">请再试一次，这个版本应该能保留所有内容了。如果还有问题，我们可以继续调整。</p><

 */
input,
optgroup,
select,
textarea {
  margin: 0;
  font-size: 1rem;
  line-height: var(--line-height);
  font-family: inherit;
  letter-spacing: inherit;
}
input {
  overflow: visible;
}
select {
  text-transform: none;
}
legend {
  max-width: 100%;
  padding: 0;
  color: inherit;
  white-space: normal;
}
textarea {
  overflow: auto;
}
[type="checkbox"],
[type="radio"] {
  padding: 0;
}
::-webkit-inner-spin-button,
::-webkit-outer-spin-button {
  height: auto;
}
[type="search"] {
  -webkit-appearance: textfield;
  outline-offset: -2px;
}
[type="search"]::-webkit-search-decoration {
  -webkit-appearance: none;
}
::-webkit-file-upload-button {
  -webkit-appearance: button;
  font: inherit;
}
::-moz-focus-inner {
  padding: 0;
  border-style: none;
}
:-moz-focusring {
  outline: none;
}
:-moz-ui-invalid {
  box-shadow: none;
}
::-ms-expand {
  display: none;
}
[type="file"],
[type="range"] {
  padding: 0;
  border-width: 0;
}

    1rem * var(--line-height) + var(--form-element-spacing-vertical) * 2 +
      var(--border-width) * 2
  );
}

  margin: 0;

  padding: 0;
  border: 0;
}
label,

}

}

    var(--form-element-spacing-horizontal);
}

textarea {
  --background-color: var(--form-element-background-color);

  border-radius: var(--border-radius);

}

/**
 * Form elements
 * Checkboxes & Radios
 */
[type="checkbox"],
[type="radio"] {
  -webkit-appearance: none;
  -moz-appearance: none;
  appearance: none;
  width: 1.25em;
  height: 1.25em;
  margin-top: -0.125em;
  margin-right: 0.375em;
  margin-left: 0;
  -webkit-margin-start: 0;
  margin-inline-start: 0;
  -webkit-margin-end: 0.375em;
  margin-inline-end: 0.375em;
  border-width: var(--border-width);
  font-size: inherit;
  vertical-align: middle;
  cursor: pointer;
}

[type="radio"]::-ms-check {
  display: none;
}
[type="checkbox"]:checked,
[type="checkbox"]:checked:active,

  --background-color: var(--primary);
  --border-color: var(--primary);
  background-image: var(--icon-checkbox);
  background-position: center;
  background-size: 0.75em auto;
  background-repeat: no-repeat;
}

[type="radio"] ~ label {
  display: inline-block;
  margin-right: 0.375em;
  margin-bottom: 0;
  cursor: pointer;
}

  --background-color: var(--primary);
  --border-color: var(--primary);
  background-image: var(--icon-minus);
  background-position: center;
  background-size: 0.75em auto;
  background-repeat: no-repeat;
}

  border-radius: 50%;
}

  --background-color: var(--primary-inverse);
  border-width: 0.35em;
  background-image: none;
}

  --background-color: var(--switch-background-color);
  --border-color: var(--switch-background-color);
  --color: var(--switch-color);
  width: 2.25em;
  height: 1.25em;
  border: var(--border-width) solid var(--border-color);
  border-radius: 1.25em;
  background-color: var(--background-color);
  line-height: 1.25em;
}

  --background-color: var(--switch-background-color);
  --border-color: var(--switch-background-color);
}

  --background-color: var(--switch-checked-background-color);
  --border-color: var(--switch-checked-background-color);
}

  display: block;
  width: calc(1.25em - (var(--border-width) * 2));
  height: 100%;
  border-radius: 50%;
  background-color: var(--color);
  content: "";
  transition: margin 0.1s ease-in-out;
}
[type="checkbox"][role="switch"]:checked {
  background-image: none;
}
[type="checkbox"][role="switch"]:checked::before {
  margin-left: calc(1.125em - var(--border-width));
  -webkit-margin-start: calc(1.125em - var(--border-width));
  margin-inline-start: calc(1.125em - var(--border-width));
}

[type="checkbox"]:checked[aria-invalid="false"],
[type="radio"][aria-invalid="false"],

 */

}

  color: var(--color);

  font-size: var(--font-size);
  text-align: left;
  text-align: start;
}

  border-bottom: 0;
}

}

 * Code
 */

    animation-name: tooltip-slide-left;
  }
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="left"]:focus::after,
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="left"]:hover::after {
    animation-name: tooltip-caret-slide-left;
  }
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="right"]:focus::before,
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="right"]:focus::after,
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="right"]:hover::before,
  [data-tooltip][data-placement="right"]:hover::after {
    animation-duration: 0.2s;
    animation-name: tooltip-slide-right;
  }
